msg:Pros: Absolutely beautiful hotel. Very elegant and stylish. Rooms are large and very comfortable. Some staff members can speak English. Near Subway Line 2 (Exit 14). Excellent breakfast. 
Cons: Hotel refused to return our deposit (paid via Alipay) when we left, citing a "problem with their bank" (no fault of ours), saying they need 24 hours to return the deposit. This seems to be their default policy. After we insisted it was returned the same day, although a few hours after we have already left Shanghai. This experience left a rather bad impression, and I would not return to stay at this hotel. I would suggest that guests check the hotel's current policy regarding the return of deposits, before they make a reservation.

name:D‚Äça‚Äçv‚Äçi‚Äçs
info:Art Deco King Room
info:Stayed in January 2022
info:Solo travelers
info:14 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 6, 2022
msg:This is a wonderful old-style art deco hotel right in the heart of the city. Mere moments away from both People's Square and the pedestrian shopping street, This hotel could not be better situated. The hotel itself is extremely beautiful - deceptively so as the outside facade is a little bland. Inside, you are surrounded by sumptuous reminders of a bygone era and the heady, glory days of Shanghai jazz and swing. The bedrooms are large, light and comfortable - just look at the trip.com photos. Everything is spotlessly clean, the staff could not be more polite or helpful, and the prices are a bargain. One extra bonus is that the hotel boasts one of the finest sushi restaurants I have ever had the pleasure of dining at. I am quite sad that I never before used this hotel, but from now on, it will be my first choice very time.
----------------------------------------
name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Art Deco King Room
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:9 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted December 28, 2021
msg:It was Christmas Eve so I got an especially warm welcome from the staff. This coupled with the ambience of this historic building gave me a warm feeling when I entered. The rooms are very spacious with a classic style. The bathtub I felt as if I was swimming in. The problem with the tub was it took a long time to fill and there was a problem with drainage. It didnt interupt the pleasure of the stay though. Its centrally located with restaurants and beauticians closeby which was ideal for me . Obviously Nanjing road is adjacent but unless you particularly want to go get something from there its best to avoid crowds. I really enjoyed the video shown on the TV which shows some historical photos of events from the 30s and 40s. As it was Christmas, it was a good choice as I often come up for weekends and stay in some ultra modern place but on the holidays I think an option like this is best.

The Yangtze Hotel, opened in 1933, should be of a small but beautiful type. I feel that the positioning of "Yangtze Boutique Hotel" is very precise and accurate, and it is more worthy of the word "boutique"~
As the third largest hotel in the Far East, it was a social resort where Ruan Lingyu, Zhou Xuan and other celebrities sang and danced. It was also the scene where Yao Li, the original singer of "Rose, Rose, I Love You" and "Congratulations" sang the classics .
The painted glass dome in the lobby transports you to the Peace Hotel in minutesüßê

The advantages of the hotel are too obvious: first, the location is super superior. The real downtown landmark People's Square is within easy reach, and the People's Square subway station is across the road from the hotel, making transportation extremely convenient. Second, the hotel's catering is also remarkable. 1933 Rose Restaurant on the second floor has the most Shanghainese accent, nostalgic style, exquisite elegance. Romantic and warm; the breakfast room on the 9th floor is in Western style. Although there are not many varieties, there are made-to-order options. If you need omelettes, soup noodles or wontons, they will be made on demand and served to the table; the lobby bar on the first floor is suitable for relaxing here Enjoy afternoon tea slowly, although the dessert taste is generally not outstanding. There are two restaurants in front of the hotel. The one on the left specializes in Japanese food, which is good value for money. The Cantonese dim sum on the right is not in the queue this time. I will definitely arrange it next time~
There are many Chinese and Western options for eating and drinking around the hotel. Overall, it is good. The overall score is not low~

This time I booked a modern balcony room through the platform package and checked in on the weekend. It was very unfortunate! it turns out! it turns out! No upgrade to neon balcony room! It's said that the neon room is full, but I'm not happy! ! I originally came here for the Oriental Pearl‚Äôs special film perspective, and the package also came with a free upgrade for stays from January to February, so I grabbed the last bus and arranged it on the last weekend at the end of the month. To be honest, I was quite disappointed in the end! Finally, I ran to the balcony of the 1933 restaurant on the second floor and took a photo to keep as a souvenir~

Suggested improvements:
1. Old facilities: Although it is renovated, the toilet is old and smells bad, the hot water comes out slowly (2 minutes to prime), and the TV cannot project the screen. It cannot be completely renewed. It is recommended not to use it as a gimmick.
2. Lack of equipment: If you open the windows and doors on the lower floors, there will be a smell of oil fumes. The room is dry and the hotel does not provide humidifiers or filters. It is recommended that such equipment be arranged on the lower floors. I have caused rhinitis and allergies after my stay.
3. Price differentiation: There are differences between the promotional pictures and the actual situation. For example, the view of the rooms on the third floor will be blocked by telephone poles, and the coordinated arrangement of the rooms will also block the view. Considering that the room is tight during the Spring Festival, we accept the original arrangement. It is recommended to sell in a price range on low floors and high floors.
4. Chaotic management: Take the two-night breakfast I stayed at as an example. On the first day there was no problem with a small number of people, but on the second day there was a problem with a large number of people. You need to order the wontons and noodle soup separately for breakfast. The problem is that ‚ë† there is no eye-catching reminder ‚ë° the pressure is on the waiter. I couldn't understand that the hotel floor If it is not high, you can use the stairs. Even using the passenger elevator can avoid the dining rush hour. info:Art Deco King Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 14, 2023
msg:The hotel I like very much when I come to Shanghai. The ancient building in 1933 was designed by Li Fan, an architect who studied in France. It became one of the architectural landmarks that attracted much attention because of its innovative design, and it was also known as (the third largest hotel in the Far East). For a while, it was the haunt of famous actors in Shanghai in the 1920s and 1930s, and the birthplace of the famous song "Rose Rose I Love You". It is very well maintained and the location is superb. It is next to People's Park and East Nanjing Road. The subway line 2 directly leads to Hongqiao and Pudong Airport. The transportation is very convenient. It is very convenient to eat, drink and have fun. The hotel itself is also very good. Shanghai was prosperous in the last century, but the almshouse is very convenient to use. The corridors are decorated with antique objects from nearly a hundred years ago. The room is very large, the bed is super large and comfortable, foreign-related hotels, satellite TV can watch many foreign language channels for free, and there are also many foreigners. Checking in, the service is very considerate, and the price/performance ratio is very high. It's super awesome. I will stay here again next time~

It is very convenient for shopping, viewing, watching exhibitions, watching dramas, etc.
The hotel is an old building in the 1930s. It was designed by Mr. Li Pan, an architect who studied in Belgium. It is a typical Art Deco style and was once famous. The interior decoration of the hotel still follows this style, revealing a strong a**osphere of the Republic of China.
Due to the decoration style of the hotel's facilities, the tone is dark, giving people an old feeling, but it does not hinder the use. Inside the room, the living and bathroom spaces are also large enough, with the style of an old-fashioned high-end hotel.
The service is average, more or less a state-run a**osphere, but it is quite satisfactory, nothing special good or bad. However, in such a central location, with such a room size and price, the price/performance ratio is super high!

msg:The Yangtze Hotel is a hotel with profound historical accumulation. The moment you open the door and step into the hotel lobby, you feel as if you have entered a time machine. The dark and deep colors and lights make you instantly quiet, and a door blocks the hustle and bustle of the road. The hotel has gone through 90 springs, summers, autumns and winters, and this unique sense of historical precipitation is really unique. The hotel once witnessed the prosperity and hustle and bustle of Shiliyangchang. After years of baptism, the prosperity is still there, but it adds a bit of history.
         From the details of the hotel, it can be seen that a lot of effort has been put into the design of the year and the renovation in recent years. The hotel rooms are very high and the walls are thick and soundproof. Even if you stay in the hotel in winter, you will not feel too cold even if you don‚Äôt turn on the air conditioner, and the temperature is suitable. The windows of the rooms can be opened, and some rooms have balconies. The layout of the room is also relatively good. The bathroom is large and equipped with an oversized bathtub. This kind of large bathtub is very comfortable to take a bath in, but you also need to pay attention to safety. The bathtub is relatively deep, and you must pay attention to safety when entering and exiting the bathtub.
         The soft power of the hotel is also relatively strong, and the staff at the front desk are naturally considerate. The cleaning lady of the guest room works carefully and pays attention to details.
         There is a small problem during the stay. On the evening of January 26, I called the front desk to ask for slippers, but one of the two pairs of slippers delivered was used. This problem needs attention, such as bath towels, towels, slippers, and bedding. Do not confuse them. These items are close-fitting items that are most likely to cause cross-infection of diseases. Be careful not to give the used items to the guests.
         Overall the hotel is still very good, software and hardware is still excellent. Some small details are more perfect when they are noticed.
         I want to experience the suite in the future.

3. Is a 500 incidental deposit required for check-in for Ctrip orders? ? Many five-star hotels in Pudong do not charge a deposit, so why not? ?
4. When you arrive at the door of the room when you check in, three or four male waiters come out of the room one after another, laughing and playing, no communication, no explanation, no greeting when you see the guest checking in. After thinking about it for a long time, I still can't figure it out. Are they using my room for a meeting?
5. The door skin on the top of the minibar is peeling off.
6. Going back to the hotel in the middle of the night, a male waiter next to the takeaway counter on the first floor looked down and swiped his phone seriously. Standing by his side for a long time, always bowing his head to study when passing by and entering the elevator. admire!
7. Going back to the room in the middle of the night, there is actually a small lipstick box behind the table? ! I thought it was a family planning supplies box! Fortunately, single occupancy, otherwise big trouble!
8. The bedside lampshade shakes badly, and no one seems to be paying attention.
9. The bedside lamp control switch sticker is rough and peeling.
10. Clothes and trousers hang in a mess.
11. There is no plastic bag in the trash can? Fortunately, I didn't generate any garbage, otherwise, how to deal with the sanitation of the inner wall of the barrel? Think carefully.
advantage:
The hot water in the bath comes out quickly, the slippers are very comfortable, and the soles are very thick. Seconds* to many five-star hotels.
To sum up, it feels like a state-owned enterprise is managing. The front desk service is arrogant and indifferent, and the room products are mottled. Most importantly, the service is impersonal. By the way, butler service? ? ? Is this family in charge? ? ? ? ?
There are many high-star hotels around, and Kempinski's entire suite is only a few hundred dollars more expensive, which is not worth it.
